  from abacusai.api_class import * # Node 1 def process_document_function(document_file: Blob): Â Â Â Â from abacusai import AgentResponse, ApiClient, DocumentProcessingConfig, OcrMode Â Â Â Â client = ApiClient() Â Â Â Â # Determine the file type Â Â Â Â filename = document_file.filename.lower() Â Â Â Â if filename.endswith('.pdf'): Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â ocr_setting = OcrMode.COMPREHENSIVE Â Â Â Â elif filename.endswith('.docx'): Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â ocr_setting = OcrMode.AUTO Â Â Â Â else: Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â return AgentResponse(status="error", message="Unsupported file type.   # Fix the process_document_function by importing Blob def process_document_function(document_file): Â Â Â Â from abacusai import AgentResponse, ApiClient, DocumentProcessingConfig, OcrMode Â Â Â Â from abacusai.client import BlobInput Â Â Â Â client = ApiClient() Â Â Â Â # Handle the document file (it should be a Blob object) Â Â Â Â if hasattr(document_file, 'filename') and hasattr(document_file, 'contents'): Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â filename = document_file.filename.lower() Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â document_content = document_file.contents Â Â Â Â else: Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â # If it's not a Blob, try to handle it as BlobInput Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â try: Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â blob_input = BlobInput(document_file) Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â filename = blob_input.filename.lower() Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â document_content = blob_input.contents Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â except: Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â return AgentResponse(status="error", message="Invalid file format.")
